Amidst Tensions Between Japan and Russia, the Red Army's Far East Deployment: Planned in Four Concentrated Areas: Taking a Large Encirclement Formation Against Manchuria 48

Vladivostok News: According to reliable investigations, comparing the Soviet Far East Red Army in 1931 with 1933, infantry has increased by 100%, and cavalry has increased by more than 150%. This troop strength is deployed in approximately four concentrated areas: (1) Southwestern Coastal Province, (2) Khabarovsk (i.e., Boli) at the confluence of the Ussuri River and Songhua River, (3) Blagoveshchensk (i.e., Hailanpao) in the Amur Oblast, and (4) Transbaikalia.

The first concentrated area is further divided into the following three locations:

(1) Vladivostok area, including one infantry division, the Vladivostok Air Squadron, the Posyet Air Squadron, the Vladivostok Fortress, and a weaker unit of the Far East Fleet, and small submarines. The main task is to defend Vladivostok. (2) Nikolsk-Ussuriysk, Grodekovo, Spassk, and Menzovka area, including two infantry divisions, the Spassk Air Group, one cavalry division, one independent brigade (?), a field heavy artillery regiment, a tank unit, and one gunboat carrying heavy artillery on Lake Khanka. In the event of a crisis, these units will serve as forces to invade the Hailin area of Jilin Province and the eastern section of the Chinese Eastern Railway area. (3) Iman area, including one cavalry division and another independent brigade (?), will serve as a force to threaten the Chinese Eastern Railway from the Mishan-Hulin area of Jilin Province.

The second concentrated area:

Boli area, including one infantry division, an air squadron, a tank unit, the Amur unit of the Far East Fleet, and naval aviation. The main task is to defend the Ussuri Railway and conduct operations in the Songhua River basin. The military headquarters is in Boli.

The third concentrated area:

Hailanpao, Chkalovo, and Blaye area, including three infantry divisions, an air group, and a tank unit, responsible for the task of operating in Qiqihar by crossing the Greater Khingan Range from the north of Heilongjiang Province.

The fourth concentrated area is also divided into three:

(1) Chita, Kalymskaya, and Bolshaya Ulya area, including two infantry divisions, one cavalry division, a field heavy artillery regiment, a tank unit, a mechanized unit, the Chita Air Group, and the Bolshaya Ulya Air Squadron, responsible for the main operations in the Hulunbuir Greater Khingan Range area. (2) Sretensk and Nerchinsk area, the units deployed in this area are unclear. A large unit of factories and the State Political Directorate (GPU) troops are stationed in Nerchinsk, responsible for the task of breaking through the border of the northern branch province of Khingan and attempting to threaten Hailun. (3) Irkutsk area, including the first infantry division and an air squadron, with the same task as the first unit. (World News Agency)

Once Enemies, Now Friends: The Leaders of Bulgaria and Romania Meet on the Danube: A Prelude to Balkan Unity 49

Sofia: Bulgarian King Boris, accompanied by Prime Minister Mushanov, left Ruse for Giurgiu this morning. Giurgiu is located on the Romanian side of the Danube River. Romanian King Carol, accompanied by Prime Minister Vaida and Foreign Minister Titulescu, welcomed them there with grand ceremonies. The two monarchs then crossed the Danube River to Ruse in Bulgaria, where there was a similar welcoming ceremony. Today's meeting between the two monarchs is the first since their accession to the throne after the European War. It is expected to bring closer relations between the countries of the Balkan Peninsula, so public opinion generally attaches great importance to this matter. Moreover, the meeting between the two kings took place in a public manner, with large crowds of people gathered to watch. When the two monarchs met in Ruse and Giurgiu, the troops of both countries fired salutes in honor of them. At the same time, the mayors of the two cities also presented bread and salt to the monarch of the neighboring country to express their welcome. Later, the two kings boarded a warship together and cruised on the Danube River for several hours.

Bulgaria and Romania were enemies during the European War. It is said that Bulgaria hopes to achieve three conditions through this meeting: (1) complete equality of status, (2) protection of the Bulgarian minority in Romania, and (3) revision of all treaties. Whether these hopes can become reality remains to be seen in the future. However, from another perspective, it is feared that both Yugoslavia and Romania are unwilling to make such concessions. Disarmament Conference: No Early Meeting 51

Davis Suddenly Returns to the U.S.

(Geneva) Disarmament Conference Chairman Henderson issued a formal notice this morning, deciding that the Disarmament Conference Bureau will still meet on November 9, stating that the Bureau cannot meet earlier due to material difficulties. (October 31, Havas)

(Geneva) Although the steering committee of the Disarmament Conference, proposed by Disarmament Conference Chairman Henderson, was planned to convene earlier on November 3, hopes for the success of this matter are now gradually shrinking. French Foreign Minister Paul-Boncour has now stated that he cannot personally attend on that day because that day is the first time the new French cabinet will attend Parliament. Since Paul-Boncour cannot attend, British Foreign Secretary Simon and Italian representative Aloisi will also not be able to attend. Therefore, all parties here feel that it will be difficult for the steering committee of the Disarmament Conference to convene before the originally scheduled November 9. (October 30, National Telegram)

(Geneva) U.S. Chief Representative Davis will depart for home today. Various sectors of the League of Nations were greatly surprised upon first hearing this news, believing that the United States must have decided to withdraw, given the hopelessness of disarmament. However, Davis denied this claim to representatives of the press yesterday, stating that his return home should not be seen as the United States no longer being concerned about the work of the Disarmament Conference. He believes that it is best to take advantage of the pause in negotiations to return home and report to President Roosevelt on the development of disarmament. He hopes to return to Geneva before the Disarmament General Committee reconvenes on December 4. After Davis leaves, the U.S. representative in the steering committee will be temporarily replaced by the U.S. Minister to Switzerland. The steering committee is expected to meet on November 9 as previously scheduled. All sectors of the League of Nations have expressed satisfaction that Davis has decided to return to Geneva. (October 31, National Telegram)

(Tokyo) The Ministry of Foreign Affairs issued an informal statement yesterday, stating that Sato's speech at the Disarmament Conference steering committee on the 26th had been misinterpreted by other countries. The statement said that it was an exaggeration to say that Sato's speech on the 26th indicated that Japan would withdraw from the Disarmament Conference. Japan's attitude had been clearly expressed during the meeting between Sato and U.S. representative Davis on the 28th, and there was no intention of withdrawing. There would also be no obstruction to the progress of the conference. The issues of the Disarmament Conference are focused on security guarantees and the right to supervise armaments. However, Japan does have difficulties with the British proposal that should be considered in the future. Japan will adjust the British proposal after the European countries reach an agreement on the two issues of security guarantees and the right to supervise armaments. (October 31, Dentsu Telegram)

Case of the "Tunan" Steamer to Be Referred to Arbitration 64

(Nanjing) Liu Hongsheng, the Manager of the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company, submitted the case of the "Tunan" steamer to the board of directors, requesting the Ministry to refer the "Tunan" case to arbitration. The board of directors approved the resolution and submitted it to the Ministry, stating that the "Tunan" steamer was sunk by the Japanese steamer "Changchun Maru," resulting in significant losses and the drowning of hundreds of crew and passengers. The company has conducted a detailed investigation and proved that the responsibility for the accident lies entirely with the Japanese ship. The company has repeatedly written to the Dalian Steamship Company, but the company ignored the letters. If a lawsuit were filed in ordinary court, it would be restricted by the jurisdiction, as exemplified by the previous case of the "Longye Maru" of the Japanese Mail Steamship Company sinking the "Xinkang." If a lawsuit were filed in a Japanese court, it would be structurally prohibited, and the court's bias would be expected. Now, after a decision by the affiliated association, it is approved to establish an arbitration committee to arbitrate this case, so that the perpetrator cannot escape responsibility and the losses should be compensated. (Special dispatch, 31st)

Liu Xiang Discusses Bandit Suppression in An'chuan 86

Chongqing correspondence: The Sichuan People's Anti-Bandit Support Association invited Liu Xiang, Commander-in-Chief of Bandit Suppression in Sichuan, yesterday at the Municipal Chamber of Commerce to announce the bandit suppression strategy and the An'chuan plan. The record of Liu's speech is as follows:

Sichuan's Governance 87

The political situation in Sichuan is closely related to the problem of suppressing the Reds. We cannot separate bandit suppression from Sichuan's governance, nor can we discuss Sichuan's governance without considering bandit suppression. They are two sides of the same coin. When the 24th and 8th Armies were engaged in discord, the Red Tide in northern Sichuan was surging. Generally, people were deeply concerned that the Tian Army could not resist, feeling that the people's suffering should be eliminated first, and then Sichuan should be secured. I (Liu Xiang refers to himself) repeatedly telegraphed both sides, urging them not to start a war. The Central Government also repeatedly telegraphed to stop them, but to no avail after two days of appeals. Having no choice, I estimated the marching time and resolutely decided to send troops to stop them. At that time, many people suspected that bandit suppression by the Tian Army would be affected, so many held disputes about this matter. However, I determined that the Communists would have difficulty advancing during the An'chuan campaign, and ultimately, as expected, the An'chuan military campaign concluded, and the Red bandits' power remained stagnant. Although some people inevitably viewed this as a civil war, I believed that the political situation in Sichuan had been completely improved by this one stroke, because it is extremely difficult to reduce troops in peacetime, but this time, 60,000 to 70,000 of the 100,000 soldiers of the 24th Army were reduced in one month. From the perspective of the people's burden, this can reduce at least 10 million yuan each year. The 20th Army absorbed the most of the 24th Army's troops, about 70,000, followed by Deng Xihou with about 10,000, and then Li Qixiang and Luo Zezhou with about 5,000 each. However, because I did not have warlike thoughts, I ultimately telegraphed the generals to implement demobilization. When demobilizing, I indeed spent some effort, and even the generals were nervous for me, because Peng and Mei had absorbed more troops than our army. I disregarded everything and ordered it to be implemented in a short period of time, finally achieving the current results. After the commanders of the 24th Army were relieved of their military duties, I gave a speech to them, stating that their past property, regardless of its source, would not be questioned, and even the property of an evildoer like Shi Zhaowu was not confiscated. This was partly to prevent the outflow of Sichuan's economy and partly to avoid the name of being a peer to Xu Xiangqian (Xu is a communist). Although I cannot be sure that all the generals have absolutely no complaints about this approach, they will certainly be fortunate that their troops will ultimately disintegrate and their leaders' property will still be preserved. When I was extremely anxious about the demobilization, the outside world did not investigate and rumors flourished, saying that the 21st Army was expanding its strength, or that I would soon return to Chongqing from Chengdu. In fact, I remained calm. Currently, Liu Wenhui's troops number no more than 7,000 to 8,000. I dare to believe that Sichuan will definitely not have any more wars in the future, because I treat people with sincerity and trust, and people will not treat me with hypocrisy. The military expenditure for this An'chuan campaign amounted to 2 million yuan, but the 11th Army used only one-third of it. From this, it can be seen my sincerity to the armies. However, after the end of the military campaign, I dare not say what achievements it has made, but the public security of the provincial capital and the tax revenues of the prefectures and counties, after my reorganization, have made the armies feel that the methods are convenient and the profits are greater. Compared with the past, when disputes over tax revenues led to armed soldiers robbing in broad daylight, the benefits are much greater. Furthermore, I have always been averse to publicity in my work. When I first arrived at Sanhepu in Chengdu, the press in the provincial capital prepared questions, seeking my answers. The reason why I did not want to answer was the same. The people of southwestern Sichuan have suffered deeply. Even taking my hometown as an example, the burden is not small every year, so I believe that it is impossible to quell the people's resentment without earnestly relieving the people.

Suppressing Bandits 88

Regarding the An'chuan part, it has been described above. Now, I will speak specifically about suppressing the Reds. Since the Communist Party has disturbed Sichuan, the armies of Liu Ji and Yang Sen have lost cities and territories, which were misled by rumors. Recently, the entire province's goals have been concentrated on bandit suppression, but many of the Sichuan generals still advocate managing the aftermath first. However, the 21st Army believes that unless we resolutely annihilate the Red bandits first, we cannot comfort the people's expectations. However, the 21st Army cannot do this alone, in order to seize all the glory, because this matter is for the benefit of the people, not for private gain. The reason why I delayed taking up the post of Commander-in-Chief of Bandit Suppression in the past was nothing more than that I did not want to wear the hat of Bandit Suppression while carrying out the reality of An'chuan. The outside world did not investigate and inevitably spread errors. Recently, Deng's army has been unable to send troops for some time due to financial difficulties, which has caused a lot of trouble. However, the generals of Deng's army have mortgaged the red contracts and have not been able to get help from the banking community. What can they do? However, it is too much to blame the banking community, because it seems useless to hold the red contracts. The armies have been seeking consent for a general attack by telegram in recent days, and I am preparing to advance to suppress them. Approximately, after the troops of all routes have completed their concentration, a general attack will be launched. At present, the troops of Zhang Huafeng's brigade of our army are in the Dashiqiao area, where there are no bandit traces. Although more than 200 Communists came to disturb a few days ago, they were quickly repelled. In the future, the military plan will first restore Suiding and Xuanhan, and then attack the four counties of Tongnan, Bayi, and Yi. It is expected that the Red bandits will definitely not dare to fight with their main force and bring about their own defeat. I hope that the military and the people will be united and create a strong anti-Communist atmosphere, then the Red bandits will be suspended in the air and easy to capture, and their original form of being unable to support a three-hour battle will be fully exposed. As for the private deposits of all gentry, there is no need to be alarmed by rumors and easily withdraw them. The Resettlement Committee has now been officially established, and there are many more matters for relief that rely on the people. I hope that similar organizations can continue to be established in various places to promote military-civilian relations. As for the 21st Army's defense zone, it is known for its strict anti-Communism, and even within the troops, the anti-Communist atmosphere is extremely strong. This Red disaster will definitely not invade. We cannot compare Jiangxi and Sichuan. I believe that the Red bandits can be eliminated within three months. Attention should then be paid to developing industries and building up local areas. The 21st Army had already laid the foundation for these two points long ago. In the future, I hope that all sectors of society will earnestly cooperate with the government to carry out these tasks together. Do not alarm each other and hope to escape. I personally consider bandit suppression to be the most glorious undertaking. If I do not immediately eliminate the Red bandits, I will be ashamed of the elders in Sichuan. If I can fully achieve the two goals of no civil war and no Red bandits in Sichuan in the future, I will have nothing else to ask for in this life, and so on. (October 29th)

Three Provinces Headquarters Instruction: Special Goods Not Allowed to Have Additional Taxes; Special Taxes Designated as Important National Revenue Sources; No Interference with Transportation and Sales, No Delaying Tax Collection 89

Nanchang communication: The Commander-in-Chief of Bandit Suppression in the three provinces of Henan, Hubei, and Anhui has issued a special instruction to the provincial governments, ordering them to direct their subordinates to comply with the instruction that local authorities may not arbitrarily collect additional taxes on special goods passing through the region. The original instruction is as follows: "It is found that the Song Department is currently implementing a six-year plan to completely eliminate opium, and during this transitional period, all restrictions on the transportation and sales of special goods, as well as the flexibility of tax regulations, are uniformly regulated. The special tax revenue is relied upon to support the monthly government expenses of Hubei, the dike construction expenses, and all temporary expenditures for bandit suppression in the three provinces, and it has been clearly designated as an important national source of revenue, with all funds being collected and used properly. This is by no means comparable to the secret pursuit of private gain by military warlords and bureaucrats in the past. Therefore, this headquarters has formulated various regulations, which have already been announced and promulgated, and all transportation, sale, and planting are to be managed by the government, with strict bans. Agencies are clearly established, powers and responsibilities are clearly defined, and accumulated abuses are eliminated, transforming private gains into public gains. Regardless of military or political agencies, or any other party, no one may take advantage of the situation to privately solicit fees or arbitrarily disrupt the system. This has been repeatedly emphasized in the records. However, it has been found recently that local troops stationed in various places, as well as administrative agencies and local organizations, often set up various pretexts to privately impose additional fees on special goods passing through or landing in their jurisdictions. Such arbitrary and greedy solicitation and brazen extortion are a serious violation of laws and regulations. Furthermore, the level of tax rates is related to commercial activity, and the gains and losses of production and sales should be considered to determine the burden. This headquarters has deliberated and weighed all factors and has made the most appropriate decisions. If local authorities add additional fees, it will inevitably hinder transportation and sales and delay tax collection. Therefore, this strict warning is issued again. In the future, regardless of whether it is a military or administrative agency or a local organization, if anyone dares to arbitrarily collect fees or recklessly impose additional taxes, they will be punished for corruption and extortion, and the responsible chief officer and head of the organization will be held accountable. In addition to issuing this instruction to various departments, this instruction is issued to the Provincial Government to direct its subordinates to strictly comply, without deviation. This instruction, one (October 28th, Datong News Agency)

Chiang Promulgates Temporary Administration Outline for Bandit Suppression Areas, Emphasizes People's Peaceful and Prosperous Life, Orders Provincial Governments to Comply 90

Nanchang communication: Chairman Chiang has recently issued thirteen articles of the Temporary Administration Outline for Bandit Suppression Provinces, as the large-scale bandit suppression has made progress, ordering the provincial governments in the bandit suppression areas to comply, so as to rectify politics to achieve the goal of people's peaceful and prosperous life and restore vitality. At the same time, he also telegraphed all commanders-in-chief and all commanders to urge its implementation. The instructions and outlines are recorded separately below:

Instructions 91

"It is found that the southeastern provinces have long suffered from banditry, and repeated attacks have failed to eliminate them, and the people's livelihood has been exhausted and political effectiveness has gradually been lost. This chairman has inspected the situation and deliberated carefully, and knows that bandit suppression must first cultivate the local vitality, and the cultivation of local vitality is mainly to rectify the politics. Therefore, the various laws and regulations issued by this headquarters have focused on the two major objectives of peaceful and prosperous resettlement, and if they can be implemented with one heart and mind, it will not be difficult to lay the foundation for people's livelihood. However, it has been promulgated for a long time, but the effectiveness has not been achieved, and it is not due to the planning is not good, but due to the implementation is not strong. Now, based on various laws and regulations, this temporary administration outline for bandit suppression areas has been formulated, with a total of thirteen articles, which should be communicated by the provincial governments to their subordinates for uniform compliance, and the commanders-in-chief, commanders, and commanders of each column are responsible for strictly supervising the implementation, so as to achieve the effect of cooperation and protect the people from harm. In addition to issuing this order separately, this temporary administration outline for bandit suppression areas is attached for your immediate compliance. Please report the date of receipt for verification. This order,"

Outline 92

Temporary Administration Outline for Bandit Suppression Areas: (1) Strictly implement the Qingxiang resettlement committee organization outline and the consolidation of Baojia and elimination of zero bandits plan to clear up the villages and eliminate the local zero bandits, and implement the division of districts and placement of offices and strictly compile and check the Baojia household registration in accordance with the district office regulations and the compilation and investigation of Baojia household registration regulations. (2) Consolidate the local self-defense teams and all anti-Communist volunteer teams or strongmen's teams in accordance with the reorganization of the civil defense team regulations and the implementation guidelines for the organization and training of civil defense teams. (3) Strictly blockade the bandit areas in accordance with the blockade regulations. (4) Build strong fortifications in accordance with the bunker illustrations. (5) Make every effort to open up highways in accordance with the route scope stipulated by the seven-province highway conference and the construction of county roads. (6) Set up a telephone network between the county and the district to develop transportation. (7) Establish a county finance committee in accordance with the regulations on the consolidation of county local finances, and implement the compilation of county local budgets and final accounts, and eliminate all arbitrary taxes and miscellaneous taxes. (8) Appropriately reduce or exempt land taxes in accordance with the disaster survey regulations. (9) Formulate various levels of agricultural revival committees or village committees as soon as possible in accordance with the rural land treatment regulations to solve land and landlord-tenant problems and rural loan disputes. (10) Set up ways to rescue rural finance in accordance with the rural financial emergency relief regulations. (11) Appropriately handle various cooperative societies in accordance with the rural cooperative society regulations. (12) Set up ways to store grain and adjust food supply. (13) Vigorously carry out literacy campaigns and increase the number of public schools in accordance with the implementation of education plans. (October 29th)

Min and Guangdong Armies Focus on Attacking Junmenling, Bandits from Liancheng Have Already Retreated, Guangdong Adds Three Divisions to Enter Southern Jiangxi 93

Shantou Dispatch: Zhu and Mao's bandits' attack on Yanping failed. The central government immediately transferred the 11th Army's Chen Cheng's units, namely Zhou Hunyuan, Xu Kexiang, and Wu Qiwei's divisions, to obliquely exit Lichuan, preparing to coordinate with Liu Heding's division in northern Fujian, in Shunchang and Jiangle, to encircle and suppress the bandits. At that time, the pseudo 135th Army Corps also retreated to the Jiangxi border. On October 13, the bandits began to attack Xinfeng Street, attempting to cut off the central army's continuous horizontal line of defense and break through Guangchang. Fighting until the 18th, the bandits who attacked the nitrate mines of Lichuan were all defeated by Wu and Xu's divisions. The bandits gradually retreated towards Shicheng, Ruijin, Changting, Huichang, Ningdu, and Yudu. Upon hearing the news, the central army further increased its forces on the Fujian-Jiangxi border, aiming to coordinate with the 19th Route Army in northern Fujian to suppress the remaining bandits on the border. The bandits in the Liancheng area, being surrounded on all sides, have also automatically retreated towards Changting. The militia led by Fu Bocui has entered Liancheng. It is learned that there are not many bandits in Changting either. The reason the bandits are reluctant to leave Changting is that behind Changting lies Ruijin, the red central district, and Junmenling, a strategic pass in southern Jiangxi. There are a relatively large number of bandits on Junmenling. Jiang Guangnai went to Guangzhou yesterday to meet with Chen Jitang, reportedly to discuss joint Fujian-Guangdong defense and bandit suppression. For example, if the Guangdong army decides to attack Junmenling, and the 19th Route Army directly takes Changting, it could achieve twice the result with half the effort. If the Guangdong army remains cautious, then Fujian's alone taking Changting will not be beneficial. As for the Guangdong army's movements, it is heard that Yu Hanmou, at the headquarters in southern Dayu, repeatedly summoned generals to discuss the communist suppression plan. Zhang Da's 4th Division is stationed in Xinfeng, having formed a unified force with Wang Zanbin's division stationed in Sannan and Anyuan. Yu also specially dispatched Miao Peinan, Deng Longguang, and Ye Zhao's three divisions to enter Sannan, awaiting orders for a general attack. The troops stationed upstream of Chaozhou and Shantou, such as Huang Renhuan in Jiaoling, Huang Yanzhen in Meixian, and Huang Zhiwen in Xingning, have all convened military officer meetings and are also preparing to attack Jiangxi. Wu Jianwen, the commander of the 5th Squadron of the Air Force stationed in Meixian, has expanded aircraft landing fields in Xingning, Jiaoling, and Pingyuan, and has also transferred a large number of pilots to Meizhou, and added two bombers to Meizhou for use. A large number of military supplies and bombs have also been transported, reportedly to be used for bombing Junmenling during the day. (October 26)

Female Workers Petition at the Chamber of Commerce, Causing Disturbance 99

After Xi Huian, the owner of the Huisheng Silk Factory near Huigong Bridge, absconded due to debt, creditors and the County Chamber of Commerce are trying to find Xi and return him to Wuxi to manage the situation. The news has already been reported in this newspaper. It is now learned that Xi also owes the factory's workers two months' wages. The first month, September, amounts to 29 and a half days, requiring more than 10,000 yuan. The Workers' Union posted a warning, limiting Xi to five days to come forward and handle the matter. After seeing the newspaper report, Xi only sent a letter to the County Chamber of Commerce, requesting that the eight dan of silk stored in the factory be sold to pay off the debt. If it is not enough, the factory's property should be auctioned off to compensate. The Chamber of Commerce was verifying the letter when, unexpectedly, more than 300 workers from the factory suddenly flocked to the County Chamber of Commerce to petition yesterday afternoon. The staff side appointed work director Fei Canchen as their representative, while the workers' side appointed Jiang Gendi, Zhang Sanjie, and twelve others as their representatives. At that time, Yang Hanxi, the chairman of the Chamber of Commerce, and Qian Sunqing, the supervisor, were both present at the meeting. They immediately summoned Fei Canchen inside to inquire about the purpose of the visit. Meanwhile, Sun Zhongjie, a member of the second branch of the Public Security Bureau, arrived at the meeting to maintain order. Then, Ji Zhongzhen, a staff member of the Chamber of Commerce, together with Fei Canchen and Officer Sun, announced the content of Xi's letter to the workers, instructing them to wait quietly for a resolution. Unexpectedly, the workers firmly refused, shouting and arguing, and the order was immediately disrupted. The Chamber of Commerce, fearing an accident, separately telegraphed the Public Security Bureau to send inspectors Sun Hao and Chen Zongshou to lead the police to the scene to suppress the situation. At the same time, the police brigade also sent Zhu Wenying, the commander of the second company, to lead a squad of police officers, and Sun Zhongjie, a member of the second branch of the Public Security Bureau, also mobilized two police officers to the meeting to suppress the situation. Qian Sunqing and other members of the Chamber of Commerce personally came out to persuade them, but the workers could not be reasoned with, and the order became more chaotic. They damaged a large vegetable table, a redwood hundred-eye table, several grand master chairs, and more than ten pieces of glass. At that time, Wang Wei, the captain of the police brigade, Jin Shiqi, the inspector general of the Public Security Bureau, and Cheng Xu, the director of the second branch, arrived at the meeting one after another, seeing that the situation was serious. After further discussions with the members, Fei Canchen went outside to announce that the first month's (September) wages would be paid first on November 3, and then other matters would be handled. The workers considered it satisfactory and immediately withdrew, and the matter was finally resolved.

Widening of Sanxiatang Achieved 100

The case of widening Sanxiatang Straight Street in this county has been brewing for five or six years, and has been repeatedly twisted, but has not yet been realized. Since Yan Shenyu came to the county as the magistrate, he embraced the determination to widen the street, and ordered the Municipal Engineering Office to actively handle it. He has already submitted a request to the Construction Department to use 9,000 yuan of land donation for road construction. In addition, the Municipal Fund and Property Management Committee allocated 9,000 yuan to the Public Works Review Committee, which repeatedly discussed the progress. Yesterday, the County Government Municipal Engineering Office held the second Public Works Review Committee meeting to discuss the issue of widening Sanxiatang. Chairman Zhang Fulin discussed: 1. The resolution of the first meeting of this committee to discuss the various projects of paving Sanxiatang Street was changed from the original plan. After re-budgeting, more than 20,200 yuan are needed, exceeding the original budget by more than 2,000 yuan. It is not easy to raise money. How should it be handled? It was resolved that the road surface and bridges should still be handled according to the original budget approved by the Construction Department, and the ditches should be handled according to the first resolution of this committee. 2. It was resolved that the houses along Sanxiatang Street should, from January 1, 1924, to the end of February, all be automatically conceded in accordance with the county's determined widening scale. If they are overdue, workers will be hired to demolish them on their behalf, and the county will issue a notice to inform them. 3. The county magistrate approved the addition of Miao Picheng, Qin Xiaopu, Qian Sunqing, Gu Binsheng, Xu Yongji, Wei Maowen, and Ni Xiangqing as members of the Sanxiatang Street Widening Committee. 4. After discussing the invitation to contractors to manage the Tonghui Road project, the meeting adjourned.

Changzhou

Accountant of Lihua Factory Imprisoned and Commits Suicide 101

In June of this year, the Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association of Wuyi County seized a large batch of smuggled yarn at the Lihua Cloth Factory in Qitaiyan. They immediately took it to the meeting for disposal and should pay a fine of 14,300 yuan. At that time, the factory said that cotton yarn brokers Li Shousan hoped to muddle through the transportation to Changzhou and did not recognize private entry. The payment was delayed. The association immediately summoned Lin Youman, the accountant of the factory, to the meeting and sent him to the Public Security Bureau for detention in the detention center on July 30. It has been three months. The case has not yet been resolved. Lin was imprisoned for a long time and was extremely depressed. On the night of the 29th of this month, he suddenly wrapped his neck with his belt and strangled himself to death. On the morning of the 30th, the cook of the Public Security Bureau sent breakfast, but Lin was completely silent. It was discovered that Lin was lying stiff in bed. The bureau, knowing that the matter was serious, immediately reported it to the county court and sent personnel for inspection, and notified the Anti-Japanese Association. The Anti-Japanese Association immediately convened an emergency meeting and decided to report the situation to the county and transfer it to the provincial party headquarters, and notify the Lihua Factory to come to the city to collect the body. The body was inspected by the county court, and the chief prosecutor Yang Kongxi arrived for inspection and confirmed that the death was indeed self-strangulation.

Nantong

Landslide on the Jiang Shore of Langshan Worsens 102

The areas along the Jiang River in Langshan, Nantong, have suffered greatly from the tidal disaster. Currently, the landslide on the Jiang shore is worsening. Local communities are urgently seeking to protect the landslide, raise funds for disaster relief, and present the case to the province, requesting assistance in accordance with the Jiangnan pond project treatment and allocate funds to subsidize Nantong's repair and construction. The Provincial Government specially ordered County Magistrate Cheng to quickly investigate and determine the actual situation of the tidal disaster and the budget for the landslide protection project, and submit it for review.

Deadline for Eliminating Opium Addiction in the County 103

County Magistrate Cheng, believing that opium, red pills, and morphine have deeply poisoned the community in Tongyi, issued an order on the 30th to all districts to thoroughly investigate and arrest within their respective jurisdictions, and to ensure that the red pill manufacturing institutions, morphine dens, opium dens, and those who manufacture, transport, plant, sell, are thoroughly investigated, and closed down and punished separately. Within ten days, all public officials will be fully mobilized to implement a complete elimination.

Pinghu

County Magistrate Zhang Sued Again 104

County Magistrate Zhang Qingze has been in office for five months and has disagreements with county committee members Chen Dihou and Chen Xunru, resulting in the simultaneous resignation of twelve committee members. Subsequently, the County Chamber of Commerce, the County Education Association, the Money Industry Association, the Rice Industry Association, the Dried Goods Industry Association, the Cocoon Industry Association, the Sock Industry Association, the Oil and Liquor Industry Association, the Tea Industry Association, the Reed Mat and Jute Industry Association, the Paper and Foil Association, the Chinese Medicine Association, the Fur Association, the Tea Shop Association, the Women's Association, the Pharmaceutical Profession Association, the Garment Workers' Union, the Barber Workers' Union, and the County Fund Property Custody, etc., accused him of ten major crimes to the province: (1) deprivation of tenant farmers' interests, (2) trampling on human rights, (3) accepting bribes, (4) hindering the prohibition of opium, (5) taking advantage of power for extortion, (6) allowing the police to harm the people, (7) engaging in corruption and fraud, (8) insulting the press, (9) violating the oath, and (10) disagreements. The provincial government is investigating and verifying the complaint. Now, the case of arresting the commoner Cao Wenbiao from Zhapu has caused a storm, and the public offices of all four districts of the county and their affiliated township offices have submitted a complaint and sent representatives Lin Yangfu and others to Jin to meet with the authorities and petition.

Jiashan

Bandits Rob Fragrant Boats 105

The Zhaotianhou Temple in Dangtan, Jinze Town, north of the county, has a prosperous incense offering season every year during the Double Ninth Festival, with ships gathering from as far as Shanghai and Hangzhou. This year, the atmosphere of bandits is rampant, so robberies of fragrant boats often occur. The day before yesterday (the 28th), in the surrounding Dang area, a fragrant boat from Jiaxing with dozens of pilgrims on board sailed into the Dang area. Suddenly, three or four bandit boats stopped them and robbed them for a long time, causing considerable losses. After the incident, the leader of the boat reported to the Jinze Security Group. The Security Group immediately dispatched a team to cooperate with the water and land police to hunt down the bandits, but the bandits had disappeared without a trace.

Yangzhou

Security Group Escorts a Large Number of Bandits 106

The first A group of the Third District Security Group in the county arrested two suspected bandits, Li Jinshan and Zhou Desheng, in Xinzhou Township on the 29th. They immediately reported to the district headquarters and waited for good news. Later, according to a report from the village guards, a bandit boat was discovered at the Jiang River estuary of Taiping Temple. Tao, the concurrent district head and group leader, led a team to search from land, and the Zhongzhen steamboat of the stationed Zhongmatou water police intercepted the Jiang River surface. They intercepted a bandit boat about two li away from the Jiang River and captured Chang Deyi, Chang Debai, Chang Zhou, and the young Chang Shengen, who claimed to be the boat owners, as well as boatmen Gao Guishan, bandits Chen Zibin, Qian Siyang, Chen, and eight others. At the same time, Wang Afu was captured in Zaixingzhou. According to the confessions of the suspects, they planned to rob a wealthy household in Xinwawu that night, and go to Xiannv Town to kidnap someone. Based on the confessions, the district group escorted the eleven captured persons and the boats to the city overnight and sent them to the county for disposal.

Gaoyou

Labor Collection Leads to Store Closures 107

The County Government of this county recently received an order to recruit 120 laborers. The county government then ordered the military and police agencies to handle it. Unexpectedly, the military and police took several shop assistants, causing all the shops to close down yesterday (the 28th) morning and send representatives to the Chamber of Commerce to petition. Later, Chairman Wang Hongzao visited County Magistrate Yang and requested their release. County Magistrate Yang released the shop assistants and ordered the military and police to only recruit and not forcibly take them. This morning, all the shops opened for business.

Wang's Mission to Shanghai

President of the Executive Yuan Wang Jingwei, accompanied by his wife Chen Bijun, Secretary-General of the Executive Yuan Chu Minyi, Vice Minister of Railways Zeng Cuiming, Vice Minister of Foreign Affairs Tang Youren, Chairman of the Construction Committee Zhang Jingjiang, and Minister of Communications Zhu Jiahua, left Nanjing in the same train the night before yesterday at 11:00 PM. As for Secretary-General of the Executive Yuan Chu Minyi, he asked the Executive Yuan for leave to rest in Shanghai for a few days, so he did not travel together last night.

Wang Delivers Remarks 114

President Wang met with reporters from various newspapers at about 6:00 PM yesterday. More than twenty people arrived, and he had detailed talks on diplomatic and domestic situations. The remarks are recorded separately below.

Song Will Return to Nanjing Immediately 115

Mr. Wang said that Mr. Song's resignation from the positions of Minister of Finance and Vice President of the Executive Yuan was decided very early. However, the successor and various preparations were not complete, fearing that it would have an impact, so it was not announced to the outside world. I originally intended to come to Shanghai earlier, but after receiving a telegram from Mr. Song, stating that before the successor to the resignation was determined, please do not come to Shanghai. Later, Mr. Song came to Nanjing, so it was delayed for another day. It was not until today that I was able to come to Shanghai. I have now met with Mr. Song twice and urged Mr. Song to preside over the affairs of the Economic Committee. Mr. Song said that he is currently busy with the handover of the Ministry of Finance and will not be able to go to Nanjing in the near future. Once all the matters are ready, he will go to Nanjing immediately. The standing committee meeting of the Economic Committee must be attended by all three standing members before it can be held, so Mr. Sun Zhesheng and I are still waiting for Mr. Song to enter Nanjing.

Wang is Not Passive 116

When asked by reporters whether there was any truth to the rumors that Mr. Wang was being passive, Mr. Wang replied, "In short, it is extremely difficult to be responsible for national affairs. My attitude has not changed completely from April of this year to the present. Now that government affairs are so complicated, the authorities often feel that it is difficult to take measures. If someone can have a better way, they are willing to take responsibility. We can get rid of it at any time. Otherwise, we should try our best to maintain the current situation. If we suddenly retreat at this time, wouldn't we put the country in a more difficult situation? This must not be done by those who are loyal to the country."

Diplomatic Policy 117

When asked by reporters about the rumors that Mr. Song's resignation was related to diplomatic issues, Mr. Wang replied, "I would like to tell you about this issue. Since the September 18th Incident, the National Government has only had one path to take in its diplomatic policy. The decision of this policy is completely based on facts. Since there is only one policy, there is naturally no such thing as a dispute over diplomatic opinions. The current diplomatic policy is to sort out internal affairs and strengthen national power before we can talk about diplomacy. Our country strives to maintain peace in the Far East and the world, but to seek peace, we must first have strength. Therefore, at present, there is no second diplomatic policy other than strengthening national power. The rumors that Mr. Song's resignation was due to a conflict of diplomatic opinions are not accurate. The issue of Japan has always恪遵with the principles listed in the July 28th telegram, resolutely refusing to recognize the puppet state of Manchuria and resolutely refusing to cede territory. There is nothing else to say. As for the rumors that Minister Luo's resignation was threatened by someone, it is also absolutely untrue."

Northeast Problem 118

As for the rumors that Envoy Jiang went to Japan, Japanese Envoy Arima Yoshi entered Nanjing to entertain, and then went north, and that Li Zeyi went to Japan, are all facts. Does that mean that direct negotiations and partial solutions to the Northeast problem are about to begin? The rumors are completely inaccurate. The Japanese envoy went to Nanjing and Peiping for routine receptions. Li Zeyi went there for private matters, and Jiang went back to his post. As for the issues of traffic, mail, and tariffs on the Beining Road, the Peiping Political Affairs Committee is a local administrative organ. All major issues are subject to the orders of the Central Government. The traffic issue belongs to the Ministry of Railways, the postal issue belongs to the Ministry of Communications, and the tariff issue belongs to the Ministry of Finance. What power does the Peiping Political Affairs Committee have to negotiate separately with the Japanese puppets? The same cannot be denied. Moreover, the postal services of all countries in the world do not communicate with the puppet states. How can our country communicate with them?

Luo Will Return to Nanjing Immediately 119

Minister of Foreign Affairs Luo Wenkan went to Xinjiang to express condolences, first to Dihua, Turpan, and Ili, to meet with Sheng, Liu, Ma Zhongying, and Zhang Peiwen to convey the intentions of the Central Government. He then met with Ambassador Yan Huiqing in Tacheng and took the Trans-Siberian Railway to Vladivostok, having boarded a ship to Shanghai, which will arrive in Tianjin in three days, and then south to Nanjing. As for the foreign reports that Mr. Luo met with Vice Chairman Karakhan of the Soviet People's Foreign Affairs Committee to discuss the cancellation of the Xinjiang Trade Agreement, it is not true, because Mr. Luo's passage through Russia was purely a transit and had no diplomatic mission. There is also a saying that Zhang Xueliang intended to fly to Russia to meet with Luo, which is even more absurd. As for whether Mr. Luo will return to his original post as Minister of Foreign Affairs, it will be decided after Mr. Luo arrives in Nanjing.

Denying Secret Agreements 120

As for Jin Shuren's private trade agreement with the Soviet Union, the government will never recognize its validity. Jin has now been handed over to the Capital Police Department for detention and transferred to the court for handling. His crimes are from three aspects: (1) According to the reports of Special Commissioner Huang Musong and Minister Luo Wenkan, Jin abused his power in Xinjiang, such as privately signing treaties with foreign countries. In the old imperial era, he would have been sentenced to death. (2) He was impeached by the Control Yuan and will be transferred to the Official Disciplinary Committee for punishment. (3) The people of Xinjiang repeatedly complained to the Central Government about illegal cases and crimes of abuse of power, which were sent to the judiciary for investigation. The prosecutor has begun to investigate and can handle the case according to law, so that Jin can be punished for his crimes.

Cotton and Wheat Loan 121

Following the resignation of Finance Minister Sung, the position is now held by Minister Kong. During the Northern Expedition in the 15th year of the Republic, Sung went to Wuhan, and Kong served as acting finance minister in Guangdong. Therefore, Minister Kong has rich experience in financial management. Today's financial problems still prioritize military expenditure for suppressing bandits. However, the cotton and wheat loan will definitely not be diverted. The cotton and wheat loan amounts to 50 million US dollars, equivalent to only 156 million national currency. Moreover, it is not current cash. However, the requests for appropriations from various provinces and central ministries total as much as 1.15 billion yuan. The proposed plans are all very crucial, exceeding the loan by seven or eight times. Therefore, the government will adhere to the original plan and concentrate on production, and will definitely not allow it to be diverted for military expenditure. As for the sale of cotton and wheat, it will be managed by the Cotton and Grain Control Council in the future. Currently, because the cotton and wheat are arriving in China in batches and need to be sold to convert into cash, the production plan has not been implemented quickly.

Pay Attention to National Defense 122

When asked by reporters whether there would be any changes in the recent political situation, Wang replied that there would be no changes in the short term. He was then asked that with the Far Eastern situation becoming increasingly serious and war almost unavoidable in the next three to four years, whether the government had a policy to deal with the imminent key to our country's strength or weakness, survival or demise. Wang replied that the government was doing its best to pay attention to this. In view of the active containment of the Jiangxi communist bandits during the battles of Shanghai and North China, we are clear that it is impossible to deal with foreign aggression without suppressing the communist bandits. Therefore, suppressing the bandits is the initial step in building national defense.

Issue of Political Power 123

The reporter also asked whether anyone would obstruct the implementation of the central government's plans due to the issue of political power. Wang replied that there was absolutely no such thing. Commander-in-Chief Chiang and his brothers all have the greatest determination to do their best for the country. If anyone can propose a better plan and is willing to take responsibility, they can step aside at any time. They are absolutely unwilling to sacrifice national strength and engage in internal strife.

Kong Takes Office This Morning 124

The new Minister of Finance, Kong Xiangxi, has been making arrangements in Shanghai for several days and is handling the handover with former Minister Sung. Urged by President Wang, he decided to enter Beijing last night and arrived at the ministry this morning to assume his duties. As for the candidates for vice minister of finance, Kong discussed them with President Wang yesterday afternoon. Kong expressed that it would be best to retain the two vice ministers, Zou Lin and Li Tiao-sheng, to utilize their expertise. However, the two have already submitted their resignations, and whether they can be retained needs to be decided upon arrival in Beijing. There are rumors that Zhang Shouyong and Cheng Shudu will succeed as vice ministers of finance, but according to Zhang, who was visited by reporters, this is completely inaccurate. He is old and weak, and under no circumstances will he take on the important position of vice minister of finance. After withdrawing from the financial world during the January 28th Incident, he does not want to enter the official career again.

Persuaded to Take on the Difficult Task 125

According to a certain important person close to Minister Kong yesterday, after Minister Sung resigned, the Central Political Council appointed Kong to succeed him last Sunday. Kong is full of a sense of responsibility and has great enthusiasm for improving the current financial situation. Therefore, even though he took office at a time when the financial situation was exhausted, he did not dare to hesitate and decisively decided to take over the job in one day. It was also said that since the resignation of Sung became a reality, the affairs of the Ministry of Finance have fallen into a state of leaderlessness, and the instability of the financial world is an undeniable fact. Therefore, Kong knew that the difficulties were heavy, and after Chiang, Wang, and Sung strongly urged him, he agreed to take on the difficult task, regardless of everything. The important person also said that Kong's policy direction should take Sung's past achievements as a blueprint, following the old ways, which may be more effective. Finance Minister Kong Xiangxi.

The burden on the people is becoming increasingly heavy, so Kong's plan to enrich the national treasury is to focus on rectifying the existing tax revenue without adding new taxes, so that the people can rest and recuperate. Continued on page 13.

Instructions for Participation 129

Celebration Method 130

The Second Phase of the Aviation Lottery Was Drawn Yesterday; Representatives from All Walks of Life Were Sent to Supervise the Site; the First Prize Was Not Sold and a Special Prize Was Drawn Again 131

The second phase of the National Government Aviation Highway Construction Lottery was drawn at Yiyuan on Albert Road at 10:00 a.m. yesterday. Aviation Lottery Special Prize Number (Photo by Gong Shuxian)

Holding the Drawing 132

At 10:00 a.m., Wang Xiaolai, chairman of the Municipal Chamber of Commerce and member of the Aviation Lottery Office, reported that today is the drawing of the second phase of the National Government Aviation Highway Construction Lottery. Silk Factories Negotiate and Resolve Wage Cuts; 45 Cents Per Day Starting in October; Trade Association Submits to the Social Affairs Bureau for Record 139

Silk factories in this city are unable to maintain operations due to sluggish sales and falling market prices. The factories previously convened a meeting of the trade association to discuss setting up a sales organization to promote sales and to appropriately reduce wages. After deducting the three items of silkworm moth, promotion, and Sunday allowances, the wages were reduced from 50 cents to 42 cents per day. Because the workers' lives were difficult, negotiations were conducted. On the 27th, the Social Affairs Bureau convened a mediation, but no result was obtained. The two parties were instructed to go out and negotiate on their own. An agreement was reached yesterday. The details are recorded as follows:

Negotiated Solution 140

Recently, because the end of the month was approaching, the two parties negotiated for several days. The investors still believe that the silk market has stagnated, prices have fallen, and the factories have tried their best to start operations for the sake of the workers' livelihoods, but the goods are still stockpiled and unsold. In this city, it has reached about 10,000 dan, and no one is willing to buy them. Therefore, they had no choice but to reduce wages, otherwise, they would have to close down. The workers also fully understand the overall situation. Therefore, after negotiations between the two parties yesterday, a compromise was adopted. Starting from October 1, the first-class wage was reduced to 45 cents per day, and the rest were calculated by analogy. This case was successfully resolved.

Submit to the Bureau for Record 141

Yesterday, the Silk Factory Trade Association submitted the details of the matter to the Social Affairs Bureau for record. The original text reads: "Submitted for the purpose of reporting the wage cut method negotiated by the labor and management of silk factories, requesting inspection and filing. The association previously determined that the silk market was declining and silk factories were closing down one after another. After a public resolution by the trade association, the three items of Sunday reward, promotion, and worker silkworm moth allowance have reached the end of the investigation period and will no longer be issued starting from the first of this month. The wage item will be temporarily calculated at 42 cents per day according to the precedents of previous years. On the 2nd of this month, we asked your bureau for approval to implement it. Subsequently, we received instructions and convened a mediation on file. Now, in addition to the three items of Sunday reward, promotion, and silkworm moth allowance, as stated in the mediation record, they will no longer be issued after the expiration date. All female workers' wages have been negotiated by the labor and management themselves. Starting from October, the first-class wage will be reduced to 45 cents per day, and the rest will be calculated by analogy. We hereby submit a document requesting your bureau to approve the filing. It is for the public convenience. Submitted to the Shanghai Municipal Social Affairs Bureau."

The Mainland News reports that as winter is approaching, US warships are leaving Shanghai one after another. Yesterday (30th) morning, four more ships sailed to the Yangtze River area. Jilin Righteous Army Actively Active; Total Number of Jilin Righteous Army Over 100,000; Puppet State Sells Opium and Massacres People 143

The Northeast Volunteer Army Support Association received a document from the Standing Committee of the Jilin Volunteer Army Headquarters yesterday, reporting on the investigation of the puppet state's situation and the achievements of the Jilin Volunteer Army, requesting review and approval. The headquarters sent Yu Jizhen to various parts of Jilin on August 19 to investigate the number and achievements of the Volunteer Army and the situation of the puppet state to facilitate strategic planning. On October 6, the officer returned to Peiping and reported the following:

Number of Volunteer Army 144

According to the announcement by the Japanese Kwantung Army on September 10, the number of Volunteer Army in the whole Manchuria was 210,000 at its peak last year, and there are still 95,000 this year. Last year, the Volunteer Army was in a group style, which was easy to suppress. This year, it has been fragmented, which is difficult to deal with. The number of battles fought last year was 482, and from January to August this year, it has reached 396. In August this year alone, 21 Japanese officers below the rank of captain died and 46 were injured. Although the number of casualties of Japanese soldiers has not been announced, there are many casualties of Japanese soldiers in each battle, but the number cannot be investigated. The Japanese military announced that the number of Volunteer Army in Jilin was more than 18,670, and a table is attached below. However, the actual number of each unit is more than twice as much as that announced by the Japanese military. According to Yu Chengceng, commander of the puppet state's Railway Protection Army, the total number of Volunteer Army in Jilin Province is more than 100,000. This number is very consistent with the number investigated by Ji Zhen. According to Manchuria Daily, there are more than 300 units of Fei Army in the eastern section of the China Eastern Railway, with an average of more than 200 people in each unit. This section alone has more than 60,000 people.

Work Situation 145

Now the Volunteer Army in each unit has two years of experience, so the work method is also more perfect than before. According to Ji Zhen's investigation, except for the two units of Chen Chongfang and Baisha Association, which occupy the natural terrain in northeastern Jilin, their troops are still in a group style. In addition, the Volunteer Army in Jihai, Jitun, Jichang, and the China Eastern Railway are scattered in small groups. The largest group has no more than two or three hundred people, and they act quickly. They either attack Japanese military camps or destroy railways. During Ji Zhen's investigation in Jilin City, the railways were destroyed five times in just twelve days (twice on Jihai Road, once on Jitun Road, and twice on China Eastern Railway). Each time, several trains were destroyed and several Japanese officers and soldiers were killed. Chen Chong's work performance in northeastern Jilin is the best. He is still occupying Raohe, Baoqing, Hulin, Boli, and Fujin counties. Secondly, Song Guorong's unit harasses and attacks along Jihai Road, and Luo Mingxing's unit harasses and attacks along Jichang Road, causing great disturbance to the Japanese army. Other small units have considerable achievements.

Difficulties of the Volunteer Army 146

Because each unit of the Volunteer Army has no source of funds and weapons, they inevitably have to solicit them locally, and their behavior is inevitably the same as bandits. On the one hand, the villages are supervised by the puppet state to establish village regiments to resist the Volunteer Army. On the other hand, the Japanese army uses artillery fire to destroy the villages where the Volunteer Army lives. In order to protect their lives and property, the people also resist the Volunteer Army with all their strength. As a result, the solicitation of funds and weapons becomes more difficult. Each unit of the Volunteer Army is caught in the suffering of having the heart to love the country but not having the power to kill the enemy. Fortunately, the puppet state's army secretly provides assistance, which can still maintain operations. Otherwise, even without the Japanese army's oppression, it would be difficult to exist.

People's Hearts in the Northeast 147

Because the people of the Northeast are oppressed by the Japanese, they eagerly hope that the national army will leave the customs and recover the lost land. Although the people have been organized into people's self-defense forces by the puppet state to resist the Volunteer Army, if the national army can leave the customs, the people's self-defense forces will surely respond everywhere and stir up the rear of the Japanese army, which will have the effect of attacking from inside and outside. If the government continues to delay dealing with Japan, and waits for the Japanese army to confiscate the guns of the people's self-defense forces, the people will have the heart to love the country, but will only suffer from being empty-handed.

Military Hearts in the Northeast 148

Ji Zhen contacted the officers who led the troops in Changchun, Binjiang, and Jilin, and they all said that during the battle of Weijiafengkou last spring, the Japanese civilian and military officials in the Northeast were panic-stricken and tried their best to be close to the Chinese and asked them to protect their lives in times of crisis. The officers and soldiers were also eager to kill the enemy and respond to the national army in order to recover the Northeast. Although there is no opportunity to respond now, the heart of rebellion is very eager. The senior military officers may be inclined to Japan in order to preserve their official positions, but the junior military officers and soldiers can rebel as soon as they have the opportunity.

Confiscation of People's Guns 149

Recently, the confiscation of people's guns in the counties along the Beining Railway has begun. The procedure for handing over guns is to use the excuse of organizing people's self-defense forces to order the people to hand over their guns and report to the government, issue licenses, and take a photo of each gun for the government to keep for reference. It will be handed over completely before June of next year to eliminate the people's resistance.

Opening of Automobile Roads 150

The Japanese in the Northeast are suffering from the unpredictable movements of the Volunteer Army and cannot be suppressed. All counties that do not have trains have built automobile roads. Other more important cities, or places where the Volunteer Army often resides, are forced to build automobile roads to facilitate the Japanese army's movements.

Seizing Railway Administration 151

The China Eastern Railway is now renamed the North Manchuria Railway. The Jichang, Jitun, and Duntuu railways are renamed the Jingtu Railway. It was officially established on September 1. The South Manchuria Railway now has a railway administration to govern all railways in the Northeast. All railways are interconnected and directly opened to traffic. All matters are under the jurisdiction of the railway administration. In essence, the railway administration is equivalent to a puppet state's railway department, and all railways have become the South Manchuria Railway's feeder lines.

Puppet State's Finances 152

After the establishment of the puppet state, the Central Bank of Manchuria was established. All donations, taxes, and rents are limited to the currency of the Central Bank of Manchuria. Even silver dollars are not allowed to be collected. Other Feng tickets, Ha tickets, Ji tickets, Jitie, Jiang tickets, and Jiangtie are all limited to being collected before June 1 of next year.

Public Sale of Opium 153

The puppet state has established an opium monopoly, with the head office in Changchun. In addition, 1,200 branch offices have been established in four provinces, contracted by merchants. Each branch office must deposit 10,000 yuan. Each branch office has several retail outlets below it. There are 40 retail outlets in Changchun City, and each outlet must pay a deposit of 500 yuan.

Massacre of People 154

Detectives are densely distributed in cities and villages. Anyone involved in national salvation work is arrested and massacred by the Japanese army. Whether they confess or not, they are beaten to death, especially intellectuals.

Establishment of Various Companies 155

Monopolizing profits, all puppet state's industries have been established as large companies to take over, canceling all small companies, such as electric companies, forestry companies, milling companies, gold mining companies, etc. The managers are all Japanese, and 80-90% of the capital is also Japanese. Except for these companies, others are not allowed to run the industry.

Colonial Education 156

Japanese has become the main subject in schools everywhere. The second subject is the Five Classics and Four Books. Other sciences that study national and ethnic thought are prohibited. Righteousness associations and Great Harmony Buddhist associations are organized to promote fatalistic superstitions and other theories to fool the people and implement colonial education.

Active Immigration 157

After the Northeast Incident, Japan repeatedly organized immigration to the Northeast. Later, due to the active activities of the Volunteer Army in various places, many of the people who moved to the Northeast were massacred. Even the original overseas Chinese, due to various special circumstances, have returned to their country in large numbers. Since the Tanggu Truce, the Volunteer Army in various places has suffered a major blow, and Japan's immigration policy has been actively carried out again.

Now the number of Volunteer Army in the four eastern provinces, if calculated accurately, is more than 200,000. The Manchurian army and people's self-defense forces in various places, although now under the control of the puppet state, can immediately rebel when the central government declares war on Japan and respond to the national army. At least 2 million internal anti-Japanese troops in the Northeast can be mobilized. However, if the government continues to delay for a long time, it will give Japan time to suppress the Volunteer Army, confiscate the guns of the people's self-defense forces, and eliminate the anti-Japanese strength of the people in the Northeast. After a few years, it will be more difficult. Fortunately, Japan's implementation of a massacre policy has created a deep hatred with the people. The puppet state's construction army has been eliminated as much as possible, and new people have been reorganized into the national security army. The officers of the former construction army have either been laid off or brutally killed, and the officers of the newly formed national security army are also in constant danger. In this cruel suspicion, a line of opportunity has been created for the Northeast, which is the most unfortunate of the unfortunate. The above are all the results of Ji Zhen's on-the-spot investigation. They should be presented together for review and approval. National Railway Freight Joint Transport Implemented Today. Unemployed Dockworkers in the Capital Block Trains. Joint Transport Freight Cars from All Routes Temporarily Postponed from Crossing the River. 158

The national railway is responsible for freight joint transport, which is scheduled to be implemented today. Joint transport freight cars from all routes have been allocated. Dockworkers at Pukou Riverside are demanding relief and blocking the passage of freight cars. Persuasion is underway. Joint transport freight remains temporarily transferred to ships to cross the river. Details are as follows:

Implemented Today: Eleven routes including Jinghu (Beijing-Shanghai), Huhangyong (Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo), Jinpu (Tianjin-Pukou), Beining (Beijing-Shenyang), Jiaoji (Jiaozhou-Jinan), Longhai (Lanzhou-Haizhou), Pinghan (Beijing-Hankou), Pingsui (Beijing-Suiyuan), Zhengtai Daoxing (Zhengding-Taiyuan Daokou-Jincheng), Yuehan (Guangzhou-Hankou) Route, Xiang'e (Hunan-Hubei) Section, etc., which are participating in national railway freight joint transport, have, according to the instructions of the Ministry of Railways, followed the interim measures for joint transport, the current general rules for freight car transport, the current general rules for responsible freight car transport, detailed rules for handling affairs, regulations on waybill procedures, detailed rules for handling, and domestic joint transport regulations, and are scheduled to implement them on November 1. For full-car freight, the limits are 15 tons, 20 tons, 30 tons, and 40 tons. Consolidated less-than-carload freight is not temporarily applicable to joint transport. If a single piece of freight weighs more than three metric tons, has a volume of more than five cubic feet, or its joint transport length spans two or more cars, the originating route must first consult with all routes and obtain their consent before joint transport can proceed.

Temporary Measures: After the Shanghai-Nanjing-Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway Administration received instructions from the Ministry to prepare for the implementation of national railway freight joint transport, it decided that freight cars Nos. 311 to 316 and Shanghai-Beijing freight cars Nos. 401 and 402 would handle joint transport. All license plates used for joint transport freight are marked with a red "Joint" character and are scheduled to be implemented today. Due to the Pukou dockworkers on the Tianjin-Pukou Railway demanding relief and blocking freight cars from boarding the ferry to cross the river, it has been decided to temporarily suspend the transfer of freight from the Shanghai Mekan Road Station and Hangzhou Zha Kou to the joint transport stations of various railways onto ferries. Freight crossing the river will still be loaded and unloaded by workers and transferred across the river. As for the Shanghai-Beijing direct freight cars, they will remain temporarily suspended. As for the joint transport freight from various railways to Shanghai-Nanjing-Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo, they will also be loaded and unloaded by workers at the Pukou riverside and transferred across the river.

Sanshan Guildhall Replies to the National Products Promotion Association 159

The Sanshan Guildhall replied to the letter from the China National Products Production and Sales Cooperation Association, stating: Respectfully, we received your letter of the 28th of this month, which roughly stated: The National Products Introduction Center of our association shipped 16 pieces of cloth to Fuzhou in September via the Jiesheng steamboat. After arrival in Fuzhou, the steamboat company claimed that the Shanghai customs broker telegraphed an order to return the goods and prohibited the consignee from taking delivery, etc. After a detailed inquiry, it was learned that the telegram was sent by Yongshengtai Customs Broker under your association's order. Such actions could easily be resolved according to law. However, considering that we are all compatriots, we are reluctant to cause social criticism and leave room for foreign criticism due to internal disputes. Therefore, we have been patient and cautious, and have repeatedly tried to negotiate amicably. However, your association has not investigated and has continued to force us, resulting in the Three North Company refusing to transport the goods again on the 23rd of this month. In summary, all the directives originated from your association, which is very alarming. After investigation, Yongshengtai Customs Broker has the freedom to operate and has no contractual relationship with our guildhall. All actions of Yongshengtai do not need to be based on the intentions of our guildhall members. Our guildhall members also have no right to control the actions of that firm, nor do they have the fact of ordering the telegraph to return the goods. We do not know what basis your association's letter is based on. As for the Three North Company's refusal to transport the goods on the 23rd of this month, we vaguely heard that it was caused by incorrect opening of documents. Whether this is the case or not does not require interference from our guildhall. However, your association does not examine the facts and accuses our guildhall members of destroying the national products association. Promoting national products is the common goal of everyone. Our guildhall members dare not lag behind. The National Products Introduction Center is competing for business. Accusing others of protecting private interests is too much pressure between compatriots. Furthermore, your association claims that our guildhall is obstructing the transport of national products, which our guildhall cannot admit. Even the current suspension of loading on China Merchants Bureau ships is a passive self-defense measure. In law and in reason, there is no violation. The various shipping companies are increasing the number of ships dedicated to loading goods other than those of our guildhall members, which our guildhall does not want to interfere with. How can you say we are obstructing transport? The government is fair and may not use one-sided words as the basis for a decision. Therefore, we have specially written this letter in response. We hope you will consider it carefully. This is addressed to the China National Products Production and Sales Cooperation Association, from Sanshan Funing Guildhall.

Shipping Merchants: Negotiations on Refusal to Load Goods from Jiangxi Merchants 160

The Jiangxi Minbei Merchants Association stationed in Shanghai sent a letter to this newspaper stating: Respectfully, we have repeatedly seen in your newspaper that the Fujian gang Sanshan Guildhall, due to the Shanghai National Products Introduction Center selling cheaply in Fujian, believes that it is hindering their business, and refuses to load China Merchants Bureau ships. Upon investigation, the guildhall not only fears that the transport of national products to Fujian will hinder their business, but also threatens various shipping companies, refusing to load goods from the Jiangxi gang to Fujian, trying to use localism to squeeze out the business of other gangs. They are currently sending separate letters for negotiation, but there are no results yet. Therefore, we have specially copied our gang's recent correspondence with various government offices and shipping associations for disclosure, and we hope you will uphold justice, warn the shipping merchants to consider the public interest of society, and not be used by one gang, and urge the supervisory government offices to interfere with such illegal refusal of transport, for which we will be grateful. This is addressed to Shanghai Shenbao, from the Jiangxi Minbei Merchants Association stationed in Shanghai, October 31.

Letter to the Shanghai Shipping Industry Association: Respectfully, recently, regarding the China Merchants, Chang'an, and Sanbei companies refusing to load the goods of our gang destined for Northern Fujian, we specially wrote to request your association to investigate according to world practice and our country's current laws and regulations, uphold justice, and order the companies to load and transport as usual. It has been a long time since then, and we have not received a response, which is bewildering. Your association is the general shipping organization, and according to Article 2 of the Industrial and Commercial Association Law, it has the responsibility to correct business malpractices. The various companies are accepting or rejecting the same commercial goods destined for Fujian in China, which is obviously unfair.
